function getreferrer() {
  var refresponse="direct";
  var siteref="";
  if(document.referrer.split("/")[2]) {
    siteref=document.referrer.split("/")[2];
    if (/google/i.test(siteref)) {
      refresponse="google";
    }else if (/facebook/i.test(siteref)) {
      refresponse="facebook";
    }else {
      refresponse="others";
    }
  }
  return refresponse;
}

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', timeoutNote, false);
function timeoutEvt() {
  var isPremium = document.querySelectorAll('.node-header .paid-premium, .group-header .paid-premium');
  var isLoggedin = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-user a[name=login-user-name]').length;
  if (isPremium.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; isLoggedin &gt; 0) {
    var noteHTML = "&lt;div class='timeoutmsg-area'&gt;&lt;div class='msgbox'&gt;&lt;div class='stlogo'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Thank you for reading The Straits Times.&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;Your account has timed out, login for full access to premium stories.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;a class='login-button' href='/p/redirect.php?q="+location.pathname+"'&gt;Login&lt;/a&gt;&lt;div class='close-button'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;";
    document.querySelector('body').innerHTML += noteHTML;
    document.querySelector('.timeoutmsg-area .close-button').addEventListener('click', function() {
      document.querySelector('.timeoutmsg-area').classList.add('hidden');
    });
  }
}
function timeoutNote() {
  var oneMin = 60000; var timeDur = 120;
  var timeoutDuration = timeDur * oneMin;
  setTimeout(timeoutEvt ,timeoutDuration);
}

</div></div><div class="group-ob-readmore"><div class="field-name-body-linked field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="odd field-item" itemprop="articleBody" property="content:encoded">

<p>SINGAPORE - Three pedestrians died after a lorry is believed to have crashed into them near Yio Chu Kang MRT station on Monday morning (April 23).</p>
<p>The 25-year-old male lorry driver, who suffered injuries in the accident, has been arrested for causing death by a negligent act. The Straits Times understands he is Singaporean.</p>
<p>The police said they were alerted to a traffic accident<span> involving a lorry, an SBS Transit bus and three pedestrians in Ang Mo Kio Avenue 6 at about 9.30am. </span></p>
<div class="ads clearleft"><div id="dfp-ad-imu1-wrapper" class="dfp-tag-wrapper"><div id="dfp-ad-imu1" class="dfp-tag-wrapper greywash" data-google-query-id="CLeCs9eI0NoCFY59vQodpzwPIA"><div id="google_ads_iframe_/5908/st/imu1/singapore_0__container__" style="border: 0pt none;"><iframe id="google_ads_iframe_/5908/st/imu1/singapore_0" title="3rd party ad content" name="google_ads_iframe_/5908/st/imu1/singapore_0" width="300" height="250" scrolling="no" marginwidth="0" marginheight="0" frameborder="0" srcdoc="" style="border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom;"></iframe></div></div>
</div></div>
<p>The Singapore Civil Defence Force (SCDF) said that officers extricated two pedestrians from under the lorry using rescue lifting airbags.</p>
<p>All three pedestrians were pronounced dead by SCDF paramedics at the scene.</p>
<p><span>According to the police, the lorry driver was taken to Khoo Teck Puat Hospital in a conscious state. SCDF said that the hospital was alerted to be on standby to receive him, which is typically for more serious cases.</span></p>
<div id="innity-in-post"></div>
<div><div id="dfp-ad-midarticlespecial-wrapper" class="dfp-tag-wrapper"><div id="dfp-ad-midarticlespecial" class="dfp-tag-wrapper" data-google-query-id="CLmCs9eI0NoCFY59vQodpzwPIA" style="display: none;"><div id="google_ads_iframe_/5908/st/midarticlespecial/singapore_0__container__" style="border: 0pt none;"><iframe id="google_ads_iframe_/5908/st/midarticlespecial/singapore_0" title="3rd party ad content" name="google_ads_iframe_/5908/st/midarticlespecial/singapore_0" width="1" height="1" scrolling="no" marginwidth="0" marginheight="0" frameborder="0" srcdoc="" style="border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom;"></iframe></div></div><div class="teads-inread" style="margin: auto; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 550px;"><div style="position: relative;"><div class="teads-ui-components-label" style="display: none;">ADVERTISING</div><div class="teads-player" id="teads0"></div><div class="teads-ui-components-credits" style="display: none;"><a href="http://teads.tv/inread-outstream/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"><span class="teads-ui-components-credits-colored">inRead</span> invented by Teads</a></div></div></div>
</div></div>
<p>When ST arrived at about 11am, a large area near the traffic junction was cordoned off. </p>
<div class="oembed oembed-video oembed-src-www.youtube.com  oembed-provider-youtube">
<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KHHPvAwJQpo" class="oembed-title">Accident involving lorry and bus near Yio Chu Kang MRT station leaves 3 dead</a><div class="oembed-content"><iframe width="500" height="281" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/KHHPvAwJQpo?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="autoplay; encrypted-media" allowfullscreen=""></iframe></div>
</div>
<p>A traffic light was toppled in the accident and part of it was wedged under the lorry. </p>
<div class="token-insert-entity-wrapper pull-left mode-embed_related_story" contenteditable="false" embed-code="477724">
<div class="token-insert-entity-preview"> </div>
<div class="token-insert-entity-token">
<div about="/singapore/it-was-so-sudden-it-could-have-been-me-teens-close-shave-with-lorry-in-yio-chu-kang-fatal" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" class="ds-1col node node-article view-mode-embed_related_story  clearfix">

  
  <aside class="group-related-story-embed field-group-html5"><div id="file-594581" class="file file-image file-image-jpeg">

    
  
  <div class="content">
    <img typeof="foaf:Image" class="img-responsive" src="https://static.straitstimes.com.sg/sites/default/files/styles/medium/public/articles/2018/04/23/yckvid.jpg?itok=_1PQfOaK" width="300" height="200" alt="" />
</div>

  
</div>
<div class="label-above">Related Story</div>
<h4 class="related-story-headline embed-headline"><a href="http://www.straitstimes.com/singapore/it-was-so-sudden-it-could-have-been-me-teens-close-shave-with-lorry-in-yio-chu-kang-fatal">'It was so sudden, it could have been me': Teen's close shave with death</a></h4><a class="block-link" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/singapore/it-was-so-sudden-it-could-have-been-me-teens-close-shave-with-lorry-in-yio-chu-kang-fatal" title="'It was so sudden, it could have been me': Teen's close shave with death"></a></aside>
</div>

</div>
</div>
<p>Nearby, three blue tents could be seen, with a lorry and SBS Transit bus some distance away.</p>
<p><span>The windscreen of the bus was badly cracked on the right side, while the drain railings on the pavement were also crushed in the accident.</span></p>
<p>SBS <span>Transit senior vice-president of corporate communications Tammy Tan</span> said the SBS bus was waiting at the traffic light when the lorry hit the three pedestrians before crashing into the bus. </p>
<p>None of the bus passengers were hurt, Ms Tan added. "Our hearts go out to the families of the pedestrians."</p>
<p></p><figure class="image file-media-original media-element"><img alt="" delta="1" fid="594469" element="1" src="https://static.straitstimes.com.sg/sites/default/files/articles/2018/04/23/as-traffic-2304.jpg" typeof="Image" width="780" height="520" /><br /><figcaption>A traffic light was toppled in the accident. ST PHOTO: ALVIN HO</figcaption><br /></figure><p></p>
<p></p><figure class="image file-media-original media-element"><img alt="" delta="1" fid="594487" element="1" src="https://static.straitstimes.com.sg/sites/default/files/articles/2018/04/23/nm-bus-2304.jpg" typeof="Image" width="1280" height="853" /><br /><figcaption>The SBS Transit bus some distance away from the scene of the accident. ST PHOTO: ALVIN HO</figcaption><br /></figure><p></p>
<p>Eyewitness Leow Jun An, 19, told ST the lorry narrowly missed him before it hit a man near the traffic light. </p>
<p>"I was stunned. I heard many loud crashes," said Mr Leow, who is waiting to enlist for national service. </p>
<p>The Land Transport Authority tweeted at about 10am that there was an accident in Ang Mo Kio Avenue 6, after Ang Mo Kio Avenue 9.</p>
<div class="obj-grid-fixed-460">
<p><img alt="" class="media-element file-media-original" delta="1" fid="594518" element="1" title="" typeof="Image" src="https://static.straitstimes.com.sg/sites/default/files/articles/2018/04/23/180423_yio-chu-kang-accident_online.jpg" width="920" height="1072" /></p>
</div>
<p>Motorists were told to avoid the left lane on the road leading to Ang Mo Kio Avenue 8.</p>

          var client = new ZeroClipboard( $(".permalink .stbtn-copy") );

          client.on( "load", function(client) {

              var text = $("#clip_text").text();
              client.setText(text);
            });

            // callback triggered on successful copying

            });
          });

          // In case of error - such as Flash not being available
          client.on( "wrongflash noflash", function() {
            ZeroClipboard.destroy();
          } );

      }(jQuery));

    (function($) {
      _data.ac =  '';
      _data.at = '';
      _data.visitorcat = 1;
      $.getJSON( "/login_details.php?t=" + new Date().getTime(), function( data ) {
        // Login &amp; Logout :)
         _data.visitorcat = data.service_type_value;
         _data.ac =  data.service_type_value;
        if (data.usertype == 'sub' &amp;&amp; data.login_id != "") {
          var st_login_info = '&lt;li class="nav-user"&gt;&lt;a href="https://acc-reg.sphdigital.com/RegAuth2/sphChangePassword.html?svc=st_online&amp;goto='+encodeURIComponent(window.location.href)+'"  name="login-user-name"&gt;'+htmlEncode(data.login_id)+'&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;'+
          '&lt;li class="nav-logout"&gt;&lt;a href="#"&gt;Logout&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;';
          $('.menu-user').html(st_login_info);
          if(data.ldapw){
            _data.at = encodeURIComponent(data.ldapw);
            var meta = document.createElement('meta');
            meta.name = 'ldapw';
            meta.content = data.ldapw;
            document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(meta);
          }
        } else if(data.usertype == "anoy") {
          var login_header_track = "if(typeof(tag) != 'undefined') return tag.click.send({elem:this, name:'click login header', level2:'"+_data.level2+"', type:'action'});";
          var st_login_info = '&lt;li class="nav-login"&gt;&lt;a href="javascript:;" onclick="'+login_header_track+'"&gt;Login&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;'+
          '&lt;li class="nav-subscribe"&gt;&lt;a href="http://www.sphsubscription.com.sg/eshop/?r=products/newsubscriptionpackages&amp;pcode=ST&amp;utm_campaign=st_subcription&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_source=web-st&amp;utm_content=subscribetext-homepageheader" target="_blank"&gt;Subscribe&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;';
          $('.menu-user').html(st_login_info);
        }else{
          _data.visitorcat = 4; // sph annoy
        }
        //
      });
      
      function htmlEncode(value){
        //create a in-memory div, set it's inner text(which jQuery automatically encodes)
        //then grab the encoded contents back out.  The div never exists on the page.
        return $('&lt;div/&gt;').text(value).html();
      }

      
      

      

      // Login
      jQuery('.menu-user').on('click', '.nav-login a', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        window.location.href = "/p/redirect.php?q="+encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);
      });
      // Logout
      jQuery('.menu-user').on('click', '.nav-logout a', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        jQuery.ajax({url: "/amlogout.php", success: function(result){
            var separator = (window.location.href.indexOf("?")===-1)?"?":"&amp;";
            window.location.href = "https://acc-auth.sphdigital.com/amserver/UI/Logout?logoutdest="+encodeURIComponent(window.location.href+separator + "loggedout=true");
        }});
      });
      
    })(jQuery);
  </script>
